if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'b11670404f09d4bafa54e4af321f933fef451d52') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'b11670404f09d4bafa54e4af321f933fef451d52') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '53dbaeb42e4e5e1935939223c19006773b16c761') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'b11670404f09d4bafa54e4af321f933fef451d52') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != 'c659dc04d651a8f1bf769cc13bb4a1484a017b8f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'c659dc04d651a8f1bf769cc13bb4a1484a017b8f') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '2744ba1942c787e259abf22cec04a937503869a9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'c659dc04d651a8f1bf769cc13bb4a1484a017b8f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'ed3973be9d3e12cbd968e7984409f6f0a1a8c421') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'ed3973be9d3e12cbd968e7984409f6f0a1a8c421') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '553d75ceb8588cf01b9a8d09139f7ae9806fdb91') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'ed3973be9d3e12cbd968e7984409f6f0a1a8c421') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_6();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js') != '085579971d41144eabcccfa68009318708d9c063') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js') !== '085579971d41144eabcccfa68009318708d9c063') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js') !== 'ba9eef621440a2bc4fc273b8fd0e662e2edb389c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js') !== '085579971d41144eabcccfa68009318708d9c063') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/000_objects/script.js');
		}
	}
